<div id="p-lang-btn" class="vector-dropdown mw-portlet mw-portlet-lang"  >
	<input type="checkbox" id="p-lang-btn-checkbox" role="button" aria-haspopup="true" data-event-name="ui.dropdown-p-lang-btn" class="vector-dropdown-checkbox mw-interlanguage-selector" aria-label="Go to an article in another language. Available in 5 languages"   >
	<label id="p-lang-btn-label" for="p-lang-btn-checkbox" class="vector-dropdown-label cdx-button cdx-button--fake-button cdx-button--fake-button--enabled cdx-button--weight-quiet cdx-button--action-progressive mw-portlet-lang-heading-5" aria-hidden="true"  ><span class="vector-icon mw-ui-icon-language-progressive mw-ui-icon-wikimedia-language-progressive"></span>

<span class="vector-dropdown-label-text">5 languages</span>
	</label>

					<div id="contentSub"><div id="mw-content-subtitle"><div id="mw-fr-revisiontag" class="flaggedrevs_short flaggedrevs_stable_synced plainlinks noprint"><div class="flaggedrevs_short_basic"><span title='Changes must be reviewed before being displayed on this page.' class='flaggedrevs-icon oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-iconElement-icon oo-ui-icon-articleSearch oo-ui-iconElement oo-ui-labelElement-invisible oo-ui-iconWidget'></span><span id='mw-fr-revisiontoggle' title='show/hide details' class='fr-toggle-arrow oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-indicatorElement-indicator oo-ui-indicator-down oo-ui-indicatorElement oo-ui-labelElement-invisible oo-ui-indicatorWidget'></span></div>
<div id="mw-fr-revisiondetails-wrapper" style="position:relative;"><div id="mw-fr-revisiondetails" class="flaggedrevs_short_details" style="display:none">This is the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Pending_changes" title="Wikipedia:Pending changes">latest accepted revision</a>, <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=review&amp;page=List_of_foreign_Premier_League_players">reviewed</a> on <i>19 March 2024</i>.</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
					
					
					<div id="mw-content-text" class="mw-body-content"><div class="mw-content-ltr mw-parser-output" lang="en" dir="ltr"><p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1033289096">.mw-parser-output .hatnote{font-style:italic}.mw-parser-output div.hatnote{padding-left:1.6em;margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .hatnote i{font-style:normal}.mw-parser-output .hatnote+link+.hatnote{margin-top:-0.5em}</style><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_foreign_Premier_League_goalscorers" title="List of foreign Premier League goalscorers">List of foreign Premier League goalscorers</a></div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">


</p><p>This is a list of <b>foreign players</b> in the <b><a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a></b>, which commenced play in 1992. The following players must meet both of the following two criteria:
</p>
<ol><li>Have played at least one Premier League game. Players who were signed by Premier League clubs, but only played in a lower league, cup, and/or European games, or did not play in any competitive games at all, are not included.</li>
<li>Are considered foreign, i.e., outside the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> determined by the following:</li></ol>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><i>A player is considered foreign if his allegiance is not to play for the national teams of England, Scotland, Wales or Northern Ireland.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl>
<p>More specifically,
</p>
<ul><li>If a player has been capped at an international level, the national team is used; if he has been capped by more than one country, the highest level (or the most recent) team is used. These include British players with dual citizenship.</li>
<li>If a player has not been capped at the international level, his country of birth is used, except for those who were born abroad from British parents or moved to the United Kingdom at a young age, and those who clearly indicated to have switched his nationality to another nation.</li></ul>
<p>Clubs listed are those for which the player has played at least one Premier League game  and seasons are those in which the player has played at least one Premier League game. Note that seasons, not calendar years, are used. For example, "199295" indicates that the player has played in every season from 199293 to 199495, but not necessarily every calendar year from 1992 to 1995. Therefore, a player should always have a listing under at least two years  for instance, a player making his debut in 2011, during the 201112 season, will have '201112' after his name. This follows the general practice in expressing sporting seasons in the UK.
</p><p>115 of the 207 foreign <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a>-affiliated nations have been represented in the Premier League.  On 15 June 2023, <a href="/wiki/Guatemala" title="Guatemala">Guatemala</a> became the most recent country to be represented, when <a href="/wiki/Nathaniel_Mendez-Laing" title="Nathaniel Mendez-Laing">Nathaniel Mendez-Laing</a> was called up and played for <a href="/wiki/Guatemala_national_football_team" title="Guatemala national football team">Guatemala</a>.
</p><p><b>In bold</b>: players who have played at least one Premier League game in the current season (<a href="/wiki/2023%E2%80%9324_Premier_League" title="202324 Premier League">202324</a>), and are still at a club for which they have played. This does not include current players of a Premier League club who have not played a Premier League game in the current season.
</p><p>For each country, the leading appearance-maker is indicated by the number of matches that he played in the Premier League.<sup id="cite_ref-blstats_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-blstats-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<dl><dd><i>Details correct as of 16 March 2024</i></dd></dl>

0;padding:0}.mw-parser-output .hlist #toc ul ul,.mw-parser-output .hlist .toc ul ul{margin:0}</style><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1097603156">.mw-parser-output <figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Edwin_van_derSar_playing_for_MUFC_cropped.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Edwin_van_derSar_playing_for_MUFC_cropped.jpg/220px-Edwin_van_derSar_playing_for_MUFC_cropped.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="428" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Edwin_van_derSar_playing_for_MUFC_cropped.jpg/330px-Edwin_van_derSar_playing_for_MUFC_cropped.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Edwin_van_derSar_playing_for_MUFC_cropped.jpg/440px-Edwin_van_derSar_playing_for_MUFC_cropped.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1050" data-file-height="2045" /></a><figcaption><a href="/wiki/Edwin_van_der_Sar" title="Edwin van der Sar">Edwin van der Sar</a> is the holder of the record for the longest Premier League clean sheet streak, while playing for Manchester United</figcaption></figure>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Portugal">Portugal <span class="flagicon"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal"><img alt="Portugal" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/23px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/35px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/45px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="400" /></a></span></span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_foreign_Premier_League_players&amp;action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: Portugal"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Ronaldo_-_Manchester_United_vs_Chelsea.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Ronaldo_-_Manchester_United_vs_Chelsea.jpg/220px-Ronaldo_-_Manchester_United_vs_Chelsea.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Ronaldo_-_Manchester_United_vs_Chelsea.jpg/330px-Ronaldo_-_Manchester_United_vs_Chelsea.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Ronaldo_-_Manchester_United_vs_Chelsea.jpg/440px-Ronaldo_-_Manchester_United_vs_Chelsea.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="768" /></a><figcaption><a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a> won a hat-trick of Premier League titles with Manchester United, was twice voted Player of the Season and is the only player to win the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Player_of_the_Year" title="FIFA World Player of the Year">FIFA World Player of the Year</a> while playing in the Premier League</figcaption></figure>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Republic_of_Ireland">Republic of Ireland <span class="flagicon"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland"><img alt="Republic of Ireland" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Flag_of_Ireland.svg/23px-Flag_of_Ireland.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Flag_of_Ireland.svg/35px-Flag_of_Ireland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Flag_of_Ireland.svg/46px-Flag_of_Ireland.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" /></a></span></span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_foreign_Premier_League_players&amp;action=edit&amp;section=79" title="Edit section: Republic of Ireland"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:TorresFinale12_cropped.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/TorresFinale12_cropped.jpg/220px-TorresFinale12_cropped.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="424" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/TorresFinale12_cropped.jpg/330px-TorresFinale12_cropped.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f0/TorresFinale12_cropped.jpg 2x" data-file-width="425" data-file-height="820" /></a><figcaption><a href="/wiki/Fernando_Torres" title="Fernando Torres">Fernando Torres</a> was signed by Chelsea from Liverpool in 2011 for 50 million, then the most ever paid by a Premier League club</figcaption></figure>
